sthātum ucitam iti bhāvaḥ nimeṣa mātram sthira citta vṛttayaḥ tiṣṭhanti ye dakṣiṇa maṇḍape atra me ananya bhāvāḥ api gāḍha mānasāḥ na te punar garbha daśām upāsate kṣaṇam viśanti iha nirīha mānasāḥ nirenasaḥ te mama pārṣadāḥ hi śṛṇvanti puṇyāḥ ca kathāḥ kṣaṇam sthirāḥ te koṭi go dāna phalam bhajanti upendra taptāni tapāṃsi taiḥ ciram snātāḥ hi te ca akhila tīrtha sārthakaiḥ snātvā iha ye vai maṇi karṇikā hade samāsate mukti janāśraye kṣaṇam tīrthāni santi iha pade pade hare tulā kva teṣām maṇikarṇikāyāḥ kati iha no santi śubhāḥ ca maṇḍapāḥ param paraḥ mukti ramā āśrayaḥ ayam niścala śriyi niścalā śrīḥ yasmin tasmin loke khyātiḥ bhavitrī iyam eṣa kukkuṭa maṇḍapaḥ bhāla netra samākhyāhi katham nirvāṇa maṇḍapaḥ tathā khyātim asau gantā yathā devena bhāṣitam a dāmbhikaḥ akrūra manāḥ sadā eva atithi vallabhaḥ viṣama iṣu śaraiḥ tītraiḥ kāritaḥ tu apade padam jahāra kasyacid bhāryām maitrīm kṛtvā tu tena vai agravedī ṝgvedī vaiṣṇavān dhaninaḥ dṛṣṭvā kṣaṇam vaiṣṇava veṣa bhṛt śaivān nindati mūḍha ātmā naraka trāṇa kāraṇam garhayet vaiṣṇavān sarvān śaiva liṅga upajīvikaḥ iti pākhaṇḍa dharma jñaḥ sandhyā snāna parāṅmukhaḥ viśāla tilakaḥ sragvī śuddha dhauta ambara ujjvalaḥ aham asmi dhanī ditsuḥ jātyā cāṇḍāla sattamaḥ iti tasya vacaḥ śrutvā kaiścid ca aṅguli saṃjñayā aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ uddiṣṭaḥ upaviṣṭaḥ asau yaḥ japet dhyāna mudrayā iti teṣām vacaḥ śrutvā sa gatvā tad samīpatas daṇḍa vāṇi patyā atha tam babhāṣe tadā antyajaḥ kiñcid vastu asti me tattvam gṛhāṇa anugraham kuru atha akṣamālikām karṇe kṛtvā dhyānam visṛjya ca kiyat dhanam tava asti iha papraccha karam saṃjñayā tat ca saṃjñām sa vai buddhvā provāca a ti prahṛṣṭa vat san tṛptiḥ yāvatā te syāt tāvat dāsyāmi na a anyathā na stokam api dātavyam tadā ādāsyāmi na anyathā cāṇḍālaḥ uvāca yāvat asti mayā ānītam viśveśa prītaye vasu tāvat tubhyam pradāsyāmi viśveśaḥ tvam yatas mama ye vasanti iha viśveśa rājadhānyām dvijottama kṣudrā kṣudrā jantu mātrā viśveśa aṃśāḥ te eva hi para uddharaṇa śīlāḥ ye ye para icchā prapūrakāḥ para upakṛti śīlāḥ ye viśveśa aṃśāḥ te eva hi iti tad vacanam tad vacanam śrutvā śrutvā prahṛṣṭa indriya mānasaḥ uvāca pārvatīyam tam saḥ agrajanmā antyajam tadā ādāsyāmi iti chedaḥ āyāhi darbhān ā ādehi kuru utsargam tvarā anvitaḥ tathā iti sa cakāra āśu pārvatīyaḥ mahāmanāḥ viśveśaḥ prīyatām ca iti procya yātaḥ yathā āgataḥ cāṇḍāla brāhmaṇaḥ ca eṣa cāṇḍāla ātta dhanaḥ tu asau asau eva hi cāṇḍālaḥ sarva loka bahiṣkṛtaḥ saḥ ekadā sampradhārya gṛhiṇyā loka dūṣitaḥ jagāma kīkaṭān deśān tyaktvā vārāṇasīm purīm pārvatīyaḥ yātaḥ sva deśam gataḥ dhikkṛtaḥ tiraskṛtaḥ pāde akṣara ādhikyam ārṣam nītvā te tam araṇyānīm taskarāḥ sa paricchadam tvām vayam ghātayiṣyāmaḥ niścitam sa paricchadam aho pratigṛhītam me yad artham vasu bhūriśas kuṭumbam api tat naṣṭam naṣṭaḥ ca api pratigrahaḥ jīvitam ca a api me naṣṭam naṣṭā kāśī purī sthitiḥ kīkaṭān gayā pradeśān sa kāñcanaḥ svarṇavān yugapad sarvam eva āśu naṣṭam durbuddhi ceṣṭayā na kāśyām maraṇam prāptam tasmāt duṣṭa pratigrahāt prānte kuṭumba smaraṇāt tathā kāśī smṛteḥ api sā kukkuṭī sutau tau tu tāmracūḍa tvam āpatuḥ prānte kāśī smaraṇataḥ jātā jāti smṛtiḥ parā ittham bahutithe kāle gate kārpaṭika uttamāḥ tasmin eva adhvani prāptāḥ catvāraḥ yatra kukkuṭāḥ vārāṇasyāḥ kthām proccais kurvantaḥ anyonyam eva hi kāśī kathām samākarṇya tadā te caraṇa āyudhāḥ jāti smṛti prabhāveṇa tad saṅgena tu nirgatāḥ taiḥ ca kārpaṭika śreṣṭhaiḥ pathi dṛṣṭvā kṛpālubhiḥ tandula ādi parikṣepaiḥ prāpitāḥ kṣetram uttamam te tu kṣetram samāsādya catvāraḥ caraṇa āyudhāḥ jita āhārān sa niyamān kāma krodha parāṅmukhān prahāsāt mad kathā ālāpān lobha moha vivarjitān mad nāma uccāraṇa parān mad kathā arpita suśrutīn mad datta citta sat vṛttīn dṛṣṭvā kṣetra nivāsinaḥ mānayāmāsuḥ atha tān kukkuṭān sādhu vartmanaḥ krameṇa āhāram ākuñcya prāṇān tyakṣyanti ca atra vai cariṣyantaḥ cariṣyanti paryaṭiṣyanti iti arthaḥ jita āhārān iti ādeḥ mānayāmāsuḥ atha iti paśyatām sarva lokānām viṣṇo te mad anugrahāt vimānam adhiruhya āśu kailāsam prāpya mad padam paśyatām iti śloka dvayam vākyam he viṣṇo te catvāraḥ kukkuṭāḥ iti anuṣajjate vimānam adhiruhya su ciram kālam mad padam prāpya bhogān nirviśya bhuktvā atra kāśyām kailāse vā jñāninaḥ bhūtvā tena eva śarīreṇa iti śeṣaḥ śāśvatīm muktim prāpsyanti iti anvayaḥ nanu kāśī mṛtānām katham vimānam adhiruhya kailāse gamanam bhogaḥ vā tatra āha mad anugrahāt iti antakāle kāśī smaraṇāt mad toṣaṇāt jātaḥ yaḥ mad anugrahaḥ ete bhukti muktī mayā prāpaṇīyā nirviśya su ciram kālam divyān bhogān anuttamān tatas atra jñāninaḥ bhūtvā muktim prāpsyanti śāśvatīm muktimaṇḍapa nāma etat eṣa kukkuṭa maṇḍapaḥ caritram api vai teṣām ye smariṣyanti mānavāḥ mukti maṇḍapam āsādya śreyaḥ prāpsyanti te api hi iti yāvat kathām śambhuḥ bhaviṣyām agratas hareḥ akarot tumulaḥ nādaḥ ghaṇṭānām tāvat udgataḥ provāca nandin vijñāya āgatya brūhi kutas ravaḥ namaskṛtya prahṛṣṭa āsyaḥ prabaddha kara sampuṭaḥ tumulaḥ nādaḥ iti liṅga rūpiṇaḥ viśveśasya dhruvam vidārya udbhūtaḥ ghaṇṭānām iva nādaḥ jāta utthāya devadeveśaḥ saha devyā sumaṅgalaḥ brahmaṇā hariṇā sārdham tatas agāt raṅga maṇḍapam śrutvā adhyāyam imam puṇyam parama ānanda kāraṇam naraḥ parām mudam prāpya kailāsam prāpsyati dhruvam iti śrī skandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe muktimaṇḍapagamanam nāma aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ mokṣa lakṣmī vilāsaḥ mokṣa lakṣmyāḥ vilāsaḥ ullāsaḥ sphūrti smāt sa padārthaḥ tathā raṅga maṇḍapam śṛṅgāra maṇḍapam iti śrī rāmānanda kṛtāyām kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkāyām aṣṭanavatitamaḥ adhyāyaḥ vyāsaḥ uvāca śṛṇu sūta yathā proktam kumbhaje śara janmanā senānīḥ kathaya tvam me tatas nirvāṇa maṇḍapāt mukti maṇḍapataḥ śambhuḥ brahma viṣṇu purogamaḥ śṛṅgāra maṇḍapam prāpya yat cakāra vadāmi tat śrī viśveśvara liṅgasya mahimā parama adbhutaḥ viśveśasya caritam vaktum prastāvayati śṛṇu iti senānīḥ he kārtikeya prāc mukhaḥ tu upaviśya īśaḥ saha ā asmābhiḥ saha īśayā brahmaṇā adhiṣṭhitaḥ savye vāma pārśve atha śārṅgiṇā vījyamānaḥ mahā indreṇa ṛṣibhiḥ paritas vṛtaḥ gaṇaiḥ pṛṣṭha pradeśa sthaiḥ ghoṣam tiṣṭhat hirādarāt udāyudhaiḥ sevyamānaḥ ca āvasat māna bhūribhiḥ brahmaṇe viṣṇave śambhuḥ pāṇim utkṣipya dakṣiṇam darśayāmāsa deveśaḥ liṅgam paśyata paśyata ete pāśupatāḥ siddhāḥ ā bālabrahmacāriṇaḥ jita indriyāḥ tapaḥ niṣṭhāḥ pañcārtha jñāna nirmalāḥ bhasmakūṭa śayāḥ dāntāḥ su śīlāḥ ūrdhvaretasaḥ liṅga arcana ratāḥ nityam ananya indriya mānasāḥ sadā eva vāruṇa āgneya snāna dvaya su nirmalāḥ kanda mūla phala āhārāḥ para tattva arpita īkṣaṇāḥ nirīhāḥ niṣprapañcāḥ ca nirātaṅkāḥ nirāmayāḥ nirbhagāḥ nirupāyāḥ ca niḥsaṅgāḥ nirmala āśayāḥ nistīrṇa udagra saṃsārāḥ nirvikalpāḥ nirenasaḥ nirdvandvāḥ niścita arthāḥ ca nirahaṅkāra vṛttayaḥ sadā eva me mahā prītāḥ mad putrāḥ mad sva rūpiṇaḥ ete pūjyāḥ namasyāḥ ca ma buddhyāḥ mad parāyaṇaiḥ ete pāśupatāḥ ityādīnām sadā eva me mahā prītāḥ iti ṣaṣṭhena anvayaḥ pañca artha jñāna nirmalāḥ pañcānām akāra ukāra makāra nāda bindu rūpāṇām artha jñānena nirmalāḥ catvāraḥ vedāḥ itihāsa purāṇam ca iti vā pañca pañcākṣarī vidyā varṇānām brahma viṣṇu rudra īśvara sadāśiva ākhyānām vā artha jñānāt nirmalāḥ iti vā bhasmakūṭa śayāḥ iti bhasmakūṭe bhasma samūhe śerate iti tathā ca śrutiḥ bhasma channaḥ bhasma śayyā śayānaḥ rudra adhyāyī mucyate niṣprapañcāḥ deha ādi abhimāna śūnyāḥ nirbhagāḥ tyakta aiśvaryāḥ nirdambhāḥ iti arciteṣu eṣi aham prītaḥ bhaviṣyāmi na saṃśayaḥ asmin vaiśveśvare kṣetre sambhojyāḥ śiva yoginaḥ ayam viśveśvaraḥ sākṣāt sthāvara ātmā jagatprabhuḥ sarveṣām sarva siddhīnām kartā bhakti juṣām iha aham kaṃdācid dṛśyaḥ syām adṛśyaḥ syām kadācana ānanda kānane ca atra svairam tiṣṭhāmi devatāḥ anugrahāya sarveṣām bhaktānām iha sarvadā sthāsyāmi liṅga rūpeṇa cintita artha phala pradaḥ svayambhūni a svayambhūni yāni yāni liṅgāni sarvatas tāni sarvāṇi ca āyānti draṣṭum liṅgam idam sadā aham sarveṣu liṅgeṣu tiṣṭhāmi eva na saṃśayaḥ parantu iyam parā mūrtiḥ mama liṅga svarūpiṇī he devatāḥ iyam etad sthāna ādheyā yena liṅgam idam dṛṣṭam śraddhayā śuddha cakṣuṣā sākṣātkāreṇa tena aham dṛṣṭaḥ eva divaukasaḥ śravaṇāt asya liṅgasya pātakam janma sañcitam kṣaṇāt kṣayati śṛṇvantu devāḥ ṛṣi gaṇaiḥ saha avaśyam naśyati kṣipram mama vākyāt na saṃśayaḥ etat liṅgam samuddiśya gṛhāt niṣkramaṇa kṣaṇāt rājasūya sahasrasya phalam syāt sparśa mātrataḥ pūjā mātram vidhāya asya liṅgarājasya bhaktitaḥ vidhāya mahatīm pūjām pañcāmṛta puraḥsarām vastra pūta jalaiḥ liṅgam snāpayitvā mama amarāḥ lakṣa aśvamedha janitam puṇyam āpnoti sattamaḥ ghṛta dīpa prabodhaiḥ ca jyotīrūpa vimāna gaḥ viśveśe paramānnam yaḥ dadyāt sā ājyam sa śarkaram mukha vāsam tu yaḥ dadyāt darpaṇam cāru cāmaram saṃkhyā sāgara ratnānām kathañcid kartum iṣyate mukha vāsa ādi dānasya kaḥ saṃkhyām atra kārayet pūjā upakaraṇa dravyam yaḥ ghaṇṭā āgaḍuka ādikam yaḥ gīta vādya nṛtyānām ekam maṭha prītaye vyadhāt yaḥ sa citrān mahā bhogān bhuṅkte mad puratas sthitaḥ sakṛt viśveśvaram natvā madhyejanma sudhīḥ naraḥ yaḥ tu viśveśvaram dṛṣṭvā hi anyatra api vipadyate viśveśa ākhyā tu jihvā agre viśvanātha kathā śrutau viśveśa śīlanam citte yasya tasya janiḥ kutas liṅgam me viśvanāthasya dṛṣṭvā yaḥ ca anumodate same gaṇeṣu gaṇyeta mahā puṇya bala āśritaḥ vyadhāt kuryāt nityam viśveśa viśveśa viśvanātha iti yaḥ japet mama api idam mahā liṅgam sadā pūjyatamam surāḥ yaiḥ na viśveśvaraḥ dṛṣṭaḥ yaiḥ na viśveśvaraḥ smṛtaḥ kṛtānta dūtaiḥ te dṛṣṭāḥ taiḥ smṛtā garbha vedanā yaiḥ idam praṇatam liṃṅgam praṇatāḥ te sura asuraiḥ dikpāla padataḥ pātaḥ pātaḥ śiva nateḥ na hi śṛṇvantu devarṣi gaṇāḥ samastāḥ tathyam bruve tat ca para upakṛtyai tīrtham kvacid vai maṇi karṇikā samam liṅgam ca viśveśvara tulyam anyatas smṛtā prāptā na viśvanāthasya samam hi liṅgam na tīrtham anyat maṇikarṇikātaḥ vārāṇasī tīrtha mayī samastā yasyāḥ tu nāmā api hi tīrthatīrtham sthānāt amuṣmāt mama rāja saudha avyācyām manāk īśa samāśritāyām savye apasavye ca karāḥ krameṇa śata trayī ca a api śata dvayī ca hastāḥ śatam pañca surāpagāyām udīcya vācyoḥ maṇikarṇikā iyam sāraḥ trilokyāḥ para kośa bhūmiḥ yaiḥ sevitā te mama hṛcchayāḥ hi ā sapta pātāla talāt svayambhu samutthitam bhakta kṛpā vaśena ye asmin janāḥ kṛtrima bhāva buddhyā liṅgam bhajiṣyanti ca hetuvādaiḥ teṣām hi daṇḍaḥ paraḥ eṣaḥ eva na garbha vāsāt viramanti te dhruvam sudhā dhāma sudhāma dhāma sudhā amṛtam kaivalyam tasya dhāma su sthāneṣu dvārakā ādiṣu dhāmnaḥ sva prakāśasya dhāma sphūrtiḥ yasmāt tat yat vā sudhāma dhāma śreṣṭham sthānam iti arthaḥ mayā eva dattaiḥ śubha vastu jātaiḥ niḥśreyasaḥ śrīḥ vasayet sataḥ tān śṛṇuṣva viṣṇo śṛṇu sṛṣṭi kartar śṛṇvantu devarṣi gaṇāḥ samastāḥ idam hi liṅgam para siddhi dam satām bhedaḥ manāk atra na mad sakāśataḥ utthāya devaḥ atha sa śaktiḥ īśaḥ tasmin hi liṅge kṛta cāru pūjaḥ prabhāvasya eka deśaḥ ayam kathitaḥ kalmaṣa apahaḥ tava agre tu yathābuddhi kāśīviśleṣa tāpinaḥ acireṇa eva kālena kāśīm prāpsyasi anuttamām asta acalasya śikharam prāptavān eṣa bhānumān vyāsaḥ uvāca rahasyam parivijñāya kṣetrasya śaśimaulinaḥ kṛta cāru pūjaḥ kṛtā cārvī pūjā yena saḥ saptamī antaḥ vā pāṭhaḥ akhila loka kāma da iti śrī rāmānanda kṛtāyām kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkāyām ekonaśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ kaḥ atra varṇayitum śaktaḥ sūta varṣa śataiḥ api yathā devyai samākhyāyi śivena paramātmanā tava agre ca samākhyātam śuka ādīnām ca sattama idānīm praṣṭu kāmaḥ asi kim tat pṛccha vadāmi te śrutvā adhyāyam imam puṇyam sarva kalmaṣa nāśanam iti śrī skandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe nāma ekonaśatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ atha śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ sūtaḥ uvāca idam skāndam aham śrutvā kāśīkhaṇḍam anuttamam nitarām paritṛptaḥ asmi hṛdi ca api vidhāritam anukramaṇikā adhyāyam tathā māhātmyam uttamam pārāśarya samācakṣva yathāpūrvam idam bhavet vyāsaḥ uvāca jātūkarṇya niśāmaya śuka vaiśampāyana ādyāḥ śṛṇvantu api ca bālakāḥ anukramaṇikā adhyāyam māhātmyam ca api khaṇḍa jam pravakṣyāmi agha nāśāya mahā puṇya pravardhanam atha adhyāye śatatame sarva abhīṣṭa phala prade pūrva adhyāya ante idānīm praṣṭu kāmaḥ asi kim tat pṛccha vadāmi te iti uktam tatra uktā anuvāda pūrvakam tṛptim āviṣkurvan anukramaṇikā tad māhātmye pṛcchati idam skānda satya loka prabhāvaḥ ca dvitīyaḥ samudāhṛtaḥ agasteḥ āśrama pade devānām āgamaḥ tatas tīrtha praśaṃsā ca tatas sapta paryastataḥ smṛtāḥ indra agnyoḥ loka samprāptiḥ tatas ca śivaśarmaṇaḥ prathamā adhyāya artham āha vindhya iti dvitīyā adhyāya artham āha satya iti tṛtīyā adhyāya artham āha agasteḥ iti caturthā adhyāya artham āha pativratā iti uḍuloka kathā tasmāt tatas śukra samudbhavaḥ māheya guru saurīṇām lokānām varṇanam tatas saptarṣīṇām tatas lokāḥ dhruvasya ca tapaḥ tatas darśanam satyalokasya tasya vai śivaśarmaṇaḥ caturbhujā abhiṣekaḥ ca nirvāṇam śivaśarmaṇaḥ skanda agastyoḥ ca saṃvādaḥ maṇikarṇyāḥ samudbhavaḥ tatas tu gaṅgāmāhātmyam tatas daśahara stavaḥ prabhāvaḥ ca api gaṅgāyāḥ gaṅgā nāma sahasrakam vārāṇasyāḥ praśaṃsā atha bhairava āvirbhavaḥ tatas pañcadaśā adhyāya artham āha uḍḍuloka iti tasmāt tad anantaram uḍuloka kathā iti anvayaḥ śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ daṇḍapāṇeḥ samudbhūtiḥ jñāna vāpī uddhavaḥ tatas ākhyānam ca kalāvatyāḥ sat ācāraḥ tatas param brahmacāri prakaraṇam tatas strī lakṣaṇāni ca kṛtyā akṛtya prakaraṇam avimukta īśa varṇanam kāla jñānam tatas proktam divodāsasya varṇanam kāśyāḥ ca varṇanam tasmāt yoginī varṇanam tatas lola arkasya samākhyānam uttara arka kathā tatas dvātriṃśat adhyāya artham āha daṇḍapāṇeḥ iti trayastriṃśat adhyāya artham āha jñāna vāpī iti catur striṃśat adhyāya artham āha ākhyānam ca iti pañcatriṃśat adhyāya artham āha sat ācāraḥ iti ṣaṭtriṃśat adhyāya artham āha brahmacārī iti saptatriṃśat adhyāya artham āha tatas strī iti aṣṭātriṃśat adhyāya artham āha kṛtyā akṛtyā iti ekonacatvāriṃśat adhyāya artham āha avimukte sāmba ādityasya mahimā drupada āditya śaṃsanam tatas tu garuḍa ākhyānam aruṇa arka ādayaḥ tatas daśāśvamedhikam tīrtham mandarāt ca gaṇa āgamaḥ piśāca mocana ākhyānam gaṇeśa preṣaṇam tatas māyā gaṇa pateḥ ca atha duṇḍi prādurbhavaḥ tatas viṣṇu māyā prapañcaḥ atha divodāsa visarjanam tatas vaiṣṇava tīrthānām māhātmya parivarṇanam prayāṇam mandarāt kāśīm vṛṣabhadhvaja śūlinaḥ jaigīṣavyena saṃvādaḥ jyeṣṭhasthāne maheśituḥ aṣṭacatvāriṃśat adhyāya artham āha sāmba ādityasya iti ekonapañcāśat adhyāya artham āha tatas kṣetra rahasyasya kathanam pāpa nāśanam tatas śaileśvara kathā ratneśasya caṃ darśanam kṛttivāsaḥ samutpattiḥ tatas ca āyatana āgamaḥ devatānām adhiṣṭhānam durgā asura parākramaḥ durgāyāḥ vijayaḥ ca atha tatas oṅkāra varṇanam punar oṅkāra māhātmyam trilocana samudbhavaḥ tatas dharmeśa mahimā tatas pakṣi kathā śubhā catuḥṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha tatas kṣetra iti pañcaṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha atha atas iti athaśabdaḥ atra liṅga prādurbhāve maṅgala arthaḥ ṣaṭṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha tatas śaileśvara iti saptaṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha ratneśasya iti aṣṭaṣaṣṭi adhyāya artham āha kṛttivāsaḥ iti ekonasaptati adhyāya artham āha tatas vīra īśvara ākhyānam vīra īśa mahimā punar gaṅgā tīrthaiḥ ca saṃyuktā kāmeśa mahimā tatas gaṇeśasya atha mahimā narmadā īśa samudbhavaḥ satī īśvara samutpattiḥ amṛta īśa ādi varṇanam kṣetra tīrtha kadambam ca mukti maṇḍapa saṃkathā viśveśa āvirbhavaḥ ca atha tatas yātrā parikramaḥ etat ākhyānaśatakam krameṇa parikīrtitam yasya śravaṇa mātreṇa sarva khaṇḍa śruteḥ phalam anukramaṇikā adhyāye api asti yātrā parikramaḥ dvyaśīti adhyāya artham āha tatas vīra iti tryaśīti adhyāya artham āha vīra īśa iti catura śīti adhyāya artham āha gaṅgā iti pañcāśīti adhyāya artham āha kāmeśa iti ṣaḍaśīti adhyāya artham āha viśvakarmā iti saptāśīti adhyāya artham āha dakṣa yajña iti aṣṭāśīti adhyāya artham āha satyāḥ iti navāśīti adhyāya artham āha tatas dakṣa iti pañcanavati adhyāya artham āha vyāsasya iti ṣaṇṇavati adhyāya artham āha vyāsa śāpa iti saptanavati adhyāya artham āha kṣetra iti aṣṭanavati adhyāya artham āha mukti maṇḍapa iti sūtaḥ uvāca yātrā parikramam brūhi janānām hita kāmyayā yathāvat siddhi kāmānām satyavatyāḥ suta uttama vyāsaḥ uvāca niśāmaya mahā prājña lomaharṣaṇa vacmi te sa cailam ādau saṃsnāya cakra puṣkariṇī jale santarpya devān sa pitṝn brāhmaṇān ca tathā arthinaḥ ādityam draupadīm viṣṇum daṇḍapāṇim maheśvaram namaskṛtya tatas gacchet draṣṭum duṇḍi vināyakam navanavati adhyāya artham āha viśveśa iti śatatama adhyāya artham āha tatas yātrā iti jñāna vāpīm upaspṛśya nandikeśam tatas arcayet tārakeśam tatas abhyarcya mahākāla īśvaram tatas tatas punar daṇḍapāṇim iti eṣā pañca tīrthikā tatas vaiśveśvarī yātrā kāryā sarva artha siddhi dā dvisapta āyatanānām ca kāryā yātrā prayatnataḥ kṛṣṇām pratipadam prāpya bhūta avadhi yathāvidhi tad tad tīrtha kṛta snānaḥ tad tad liṅga kṛta arcanaḥ maunena yātrām kurvāṇaḥ phalam prāpnoti yātrikaḥ oṅkāram prathamam paśyet matsya udaryām kṛta udakaḥ triviṣṭapam mahādevam tatas vai kṛttivāsasam ratneśam ca atha candreśam kedāram ca tatas vrajet jñāna vāpīm iti śloka uktam caturtham tatas iti pāda uktam pañcamam iti eṣā pañcatīrthikā iti pūrva ukta rūpā vā dharmeśvaram ca vīreśam gacchet kāmeśvaram tatas viśvakarmeśvaram ca atha maṇikarṇīśvaram tatas avimukteśvaram dṛṣṭvā tatas viśveśam arcayet eṣā yātrā prayatnena kartavyā kṣetra vāsinā yaḥ tu kṣetram uṣitvā tu na etām yātrām samācaret vighnāḥ tasya upatiṣṭhante kṣetra uccāṭana sūcakāḥ aṣṭa āyatana yātrā anyā kartavyā vighna śāntaye dakṣeśaḥ pārvatīśaḥ ca tathā paśupatīśvaraḥ gaṅgeśaḥ narmadeśaḥ ca gabhastīśaḥ satīśvaraḥ aṣṭamaḥ tārakeśaḥ ca pratyaṣṭami viśeṣataḥ dṛśyāni etāni liṅgāni mahā pāpa upaśāntaye aparā api śubhā yātrā yogakṣema karī sadā śaila īśam prathamam vīkṣya varaṇā snāna pūrvakam snānam tu saṅgame kṛtvā draṣṭavyaḥ saṅgameśvaraḥ sva līna tīrthe su snātaḥ paśyet sva līnam īśvaram snātvā mandākinītīrthe draṣṭavyaḥ madhyameśvaraḥ paśyet hiraṇyagarbha īśam tatra tīrthe kṛta udakaḥ maṇikarṇya tatas snātvā paśyet īśānam īśvaram kāpileyahade snātvā vīkṣeta vṛṣabhadhvajam upaśānta śivam paśyet tad kūpa vihita udakaḥ pañcacūḍāhade snātvā jyeṣṭhasthānam tatas arcayet devasya agre tu yā vāpī tatra upasparśane kṛte śukreśvaram tatas paśyet tad kūpa vihita udakaḥ daṇḍakhāte tatas snātvā vyāghra īśam pūjayet tatas śaunakeśvara kuṇḍe tu snānam kṛtvā tatas arcayet jambukeśam mahā liṅgam kṛtvā yātrām imām naraḥ kvacid na jāyate bhūyas saṃsāre duḥkha sāgare samārabhya pratipadam yāvat kṛṣṇā caturdaśī imām yātrām naraḥ kṛtvā na bhūyas api abhijāyate anyā yātrā prakartavyā ekādaśa āyatana udbhavā āgnīdhra kuṇḍe su snātaḥ paśyet āgnīdhram īśvaram urvaśīśam tatas gacchet tatas tu nakulīśvaram āṣāḍhīśam tatas dṛṣṭvā bhāra bhūta īśvaram tatas lāṅgalīśam atha ālokya tatas tu tripurāntakam tatas manaḥprakāma īśam prītikeśam atho vrajet madālaseśvaram tasmāt tilaparṇeśvaram tatas yātrā ekādaśa liṅgānām eṣā kāryā prayatnataḥ imām yātrām prakurvāṇaḥ rudra tvam prāpnuyāt naraḥ antar param pravakṣyāmi gaurīyātrām anuttamān śuklapakṣe tṛtīyāyām yā yātrā viṣvak ṛddhi dā eṣa ca asau kramaḥ ca iti etad āyatanāni pūrva ukta śaileśa ādi āśritāni jyeṣṭhāvāpyām naraḥ snātvā jyeṣṭhām gaurīm samarcayet saubhāgyagaurī sampūjyā jñāna vāpyām kṛta udakaiḥ tatas śṛṅgāragaurīm ca tatra eva ca kṛta udakaḥ snātvā viśālagaṅgāyām viśālākṣīm tatas vrajet snātvā bhavānītīrthe atha bhavānīm paripūjayet tatas gacchet mahālakṣmīm sthira lakṣmī samṛddhaye imām yātrām naraḥ kṛtvā kṣetre asmin mukti janmani kuryāt prati caturthī iha yātrām vighneśituḥ sadā brāhmaṇebhyaḥ tad uddeśāt deyāḥ vai modakāḥ modakāḥ mude bhaume bhairavayātrā ca kāryā pātaka hāriṇī ravivāre raveḥ yātrā ṣaṣṭhyām vā ravi saṃyuji navamyām athavā aṣṭamyām caṇḍīyātrā śubhā matā prātar snānam vidhāya ādau natvā pañca vināyakān namaskṛtvā atha viśveśam sthitvā nirvāṇa maṇḍape antargṛhasya yātrām vai kariṣye agha ogha śāntaye gṛhītvā niyamam ca iti gatvā atha maṇikarṇikām snātvā maunena ca āgatya maṇikarṇīśam arcayet kambala aśvatarau natvā vāsuki īśam praṇamya ca parvata īśam tatas dṛṣṭvā gaṅgā keśavam api atha tatas tu lalitām dṛṣṭvā jarāsandha īśvaram tatas brahmeśvaram tatas natvā natvā agastīśvaram tatas kaśyapa īśam namaskṛtya namaskṛtya hari keśa vanam hari keśa vanam tatas vaidya nātham tatas dṛṣṭvā dhruva īśam atha vīkṣya ca asthi kṣepa taḍāge ca dṛṣṭvā vai kīkaseśvaram bhāra bhūtam tatas natvā citragupta īśvaram tatas citraghaṇṭām praṇamya atha tatas paśupati īśvaram pitāmaheśvaram gatvā tatas tu kalaśeśvaram candreśaḥ tu atha vīreśaḥ vidyeśaḥ agnīśaḥ eva ca senāvināyakaḥ ca atha dravṭavyaḥ sarva vighna hṛt vasiṣṭha vāmadevau ca mūrti rūpa dharau ubhau draṣṭavyau yatnataḥ kāśyām mahā vighna vināśinau sīmā vināyakam ca atha karuṇeśam tatas vrajet trisandhyeśaḥ viśālākṣī dharmeśaḥ viśvabāhukā āśāvināyakaḥ ca atha vṛddhādityaḥ tatas punar caturvaktra īśvaram liṅgam brāhmīśaḥ tu tatas paras tatas manaḥprakāmeśaḥ īśāneśaḥ tatas param caṇḍī caṇḍeśvarau dṛśyau bhavānī śaṅkarau tatas duṣṭim praṇamya ca tatas rājarāja īśam arcayet lāṅgalīśaḥ tatas abhyarcyaḥ tatas tu nakuli īśvaraḥ parānneśam atho natvā paradravyeśvaram tatas pratigraheśvaram vā api niṣkalaṅkeśam eva ca gaṅgeśaḥ abhyarcyaḥ tatas jñāna vāpyām snānam samācaret nandikeśam tārakeśam mahākāleśvaram tatas daṇḍapāṇim maheśam ca mokṣeśam praṇamet tatas vīrabhadra īśvaram natvā avimukteśvaram tatas vināyakān tatas pañca viśvanātham tatas vrajet antargṛhasya yātrā iyam yathāvat yā mayā kṛtā nyūna atiriktayā śambhuḥ prīyatām anayā vibhuḥ iti mantram samuccārya kṣaṇam vai mukti maṇḍape viśramya yāyāt bhavanam niṣpāpaḥ puṇyavān naraḥ samprāpya vāsaram viṣṇoḥ viṣṇutīrtheṣu sarvatas kāryā yātrā prayatnena mahā puṇya samṛddhaye duḥkham rudra piśāca tvam na bhavet yasya pūjanāt śraddhā pūrvam imāḥ yātrāḥ kartavyāḥ kṣetra vāsibhiḥ parvasu api viśeṣeṇa kāryāḥ yātrāḥ ca sarvatas na vandhyam divasam kuryāt vinā yātrām kvacid kṛtī yasya vandhyam dinam yātam kāśyām nivasataḥ sataḥ sa daṣṭaḥ kālasarpeṇa sa dṛṣṭaḥ mṛtyunā sphuṭam sa muṣṭaḥ tatra divase viśveśaḥ yatra na īkṣitaḥ maṇikartyām tu yaḥ snātaḥ yaḥ viśveśam niraikṣata satyam satyam punar satyam satyam satyam punar punar dṛśyaḥ viśveśvaraḥ nityam snātavyā maṇikarṇikā vyāsaḥ uvāca sūta skāndam idam śrutvā kāśīmāhātmyam uttamam snātvā sarvāṇi tīrthāni yat śreyaḥ samupārjyate kāśīkhaṇḍasya śravaṇāt tat syāt sūta na saṃśayaḥ da tvā dānāni sarvāṇi kṛtvā yajñān anekaśas śravaṇāt asya khaṇḍasya labhate tat na saṃśayaḥ adhītya caturaḥ vedān sa aṅgān yat phalam āpyate kāśīkhaṇḍam samākarṇya tad phalam labhyate naraiḥ gayāyām śrāddha dānāt ca yathā tṛpyanti pūrvajāḥ tathā etad śravaṇāt nṛṇām tṛpnuvanti pitāmahāḥ taiḥ ca sarva purāṇāni śrutāni sthira buddhibhiḥ kāśīkhaṇḍam śrutam yaiḥ ca sarveṣām śreyasām padam sarva dharmāḥ taiḥ mahā puṇya eka rāśibhiḥ śrutam yaiḥ sthira cetobhiḥ kāśīmāhātmyam uttamam japet tat khaṇḍam akhilam śrotavyam śraddhayā dvijāḥ śṛṇuyāt ekam api yaḥ ākhyānam kāśi khaṇḍa jam śrutāni tena sarvāṇi dharma śāstrāṇi asaṃśayam kāraṇam sarva kāma āpteḥ kāśīkhaṇḍam idam smṛtam etad śravaṇataḥ puṃsām kaivalyam nā eva dūratas prīṇanti amartyāḥ sarve api brahma viṣṇu śiva ādayaḥ hṛṣṭaḥ sarvaḥ bhavet eva bhūta grāmaḥ caturvidhaḥ mahima śravaṇāt asmāt vārāṇasyāḥ na saṃśayaḥ pāda mātram tad ardham vā tu ekam vyākhyānam uttamam tasmin tuṣṭe hi san tuṣṭaḥ viśveśaḥ na atra saṃśayaḥ yatra etat paṭhyate khaṇḍam parānanda samāśrayam yaḥ idam śṛṇuyāt vidvān yaḥ ca idam śrāvayet sudhīḥ yaḥ paṭhet api puṇya ātmā te sarve rudra mūrtayaḥ akhilāni purāṇāni tena dattāni na a anyathā atra ākhyānāni yāvanti ślokāḥ yāvantaḥ eva hi tathā padāni yāvanti varṇāḥ yāvantaḥ eva hi yāvanti api ca mātrāṇi yāvatyaḥ pada paṅktayaḥ guṇe sūtrāṇi yāvanti yāvantaḥ paṭa tantavaḥ tāvat yuga sahastrāṇi dātā svarge mahīyate etat dvādaśa kṛtvas yaḥ śṛṇuyāt khaṇḍam uttamam aputraḥ śṛṇuyāt yaḥ tu su snātaḥ śraddhayā anvitaḥ yaḥ yaḥ tam tam sa sa sadā śrutyā etat prāpnuyāt kṛtī śṛṇuyāt dūra deśe api yaḥ kāśīkhaṇḍam uttamam sa kāśī vāsa puṇyasya bhājanam syāt śiva ājñayā saubhāgyam ca api sarvatra prāpnuyāt nirmala āśayaḥ sarveṣām maṅgalānām ca mahā maṅgalam uttamam iti śrī skandapurāṇe kāśīkhaṇḍe anukramaṇikā nāma śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptam ca idam kāśīkhaṇḍam bhakta icchā upātta dehāya kṛṣṇāya haraye namaḥ nyāye kāṇādavartmani atha ca gurutaraḥ gautamaḥ vā akṣapādaḥ sāṃkhye yaḥ devahūti ātmajaḥ iva hi tathā vāsukiḥ yoga śāstre prākkāṇḍe bhaṭṭa tulyaḥ sa jayati paramaḥ śrī surendraḥ guruḥ naḥ vedānte atha purāṇa bhārata vidhau śrī satyavatī ātmajaḥ sāṃkhye śrī kapilaḥ kaṇādaḥ iha yaḥ vaiśeṣike gautamaḥ bhaṭṭa ācārya caturbhujaḥ vijayate prāk kāṇḍa kaumārilaḥ sakośā ca vikośā ca dve ṭīke likhite mayā yatra yasya abhilāṣaḥ syāt sā tena parigṛhyatām āsīt kaśyapa vaṃśa bhūṣaṇaṃmaṇiḥ mānyaḥ mukunda priyaḥ stenā iyam vihitā hitāya viduṣām ṭīkā budhaiḥ vīkṣyatām kāśyām śrī puruṣottamena viduṣā bhaṭṭena śuddha ātmanā tantra adhyātma purāṇa bhārata vida upāsya upakaṃsāriṇā rāmānanda muni indra varya kṛtayā gūḍha arthayā ṭīkayā samyak saṅkalitam hitāya viduṣām śrī kāśikhaṇḍam mahat na vana apara paryāyeṇa rāmānandena kṛtāyām kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkāyām śatatamaḥ adhyāyaḥ samāptā ca iyam kāśīkhaṇḍa ṭīkā dohā kāśīkhaṇḍa punīta yaha karata su maṃgala vṛddhi san pūrṇa ānanda saṃskṛta
